Abstract: In this article, we consider a class of incompressible stochastic third-grade
fluids (non-Newtonian fluids) equations on two- as well as three-dimensional
Poincar\'e domains $\mathcal{O}$ (which may be bounded or unbounded). Our aims
are to study the well-posedness and asymptotic analysis for the solutions of
the underlying system. Firstly, we prove that the underlying system defined on
$\mathcal{O}$ has a unique weak solution (in the analytic sense) under
Dirichlet boundary condition and it also generates random dynamical system
$\Psi$. Secondly, we consider the underlying system on bounded domains. Using
the compact Sobolev embedding $\mathbb{H}^1(\mathcal{O})
\hookrightarrow\mathbb{L}^2(\mathcal{O})$, we prove the existence of a unique

forcing in

Thirdly, we consider the underlying system on unbounded Poincar\'e domains with
external forcing in $\mathbb{L}^{2}(\mathcal{O})$ and show the existence of a
unique random attractor. In order to obtain the existence of a unique random
attractor on unbounded domains, due to the lack of compact Sobolev embedding
$\mathbb{H}^1(\mathcal{O}) \hookrightarrow\mathbb{H}^2(\mathcal{O})$, we use
the uniform-tail estimates method which helps us to demonstrate the asymptotic
compactness of $\Psi$.
  Note that due to the presence of several nonlinear terms in the underlying
system, we are not able to use the energy equality method to obtain the
asymptotic compactness of $\Psi$ in unbounded domains, which makes the analysis
of this work in unbounded domains more difficult and interesting. Finally, as a
consequence of the existence of random attractors, we address the existence of
invariant measures for underlying system.

*Vjekoslav Kovač,Florian Luca*

Main category: math.NT

TL;DR: 论文研究了函数f(n) = Στ(2^k-1)的比值f(2n)/f(n)的无界性，并给出了该序列趋于无穷的条件结果，同时通过数值实验验证了猜想和条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受Paul Erdős问题的启发，研究f(2n)/f(n)的无界性及其趋于无穷的条件。

Method: 通过数学分析和条件推导，研究f(2n)/f(n)的性质，并通过数值实验验证。

Result: 证明了f(2n)/f(n)是无界的，并给出了其趋于无穷的充分条件。

Conclusion: 数值实验支持了猜想和条件的有效性，为进一步研究提供了基础。

Abstract: Denote $f(n):=\sum_{1\le k\le n} \tau(2^k-1)$, where $\tau$ is the number of
divisors function. Motivated by a question of Paul Erd\H{o}s, we show that the
sequence of ratios $f(2n)/f(n)$ is unbounded. We also present conditional
results on the divergence of this sequence to infinity. Finally, we test
numerically both the conjecture $f(2n)/f(n)\to\infty$ and our sufficient
conditions for it to hold.

</details>


### [123] [Refinements on higher order Weil-Oesterlé bounds via a Serre type argument](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.05212)
*Emmanuel Hallouin,Philippe Moustrou,Marc Perret*

Main category: math.NT

TL;DR: 本文结合Serre的算术约束方法和Hallouin-Perret的半定规划方法，改进了Ihara的曲线点数上界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Weil定理和Ihara-Oesterlé的改进是有限域曲线点数上界的经典结果，但仍有优化空间。本文旨在结合Serre的算术约束方法，进一步改进Ihara的界。

Method: 通过类似Serre的算术约束方法，结合半定规划序列，提出了一种改进Ihara上界的新方法。

Result: 新方法在Ihara界原本最优的范围内也能实现改进。

Conclusion: 本文成功结合两种方法改进了Ihara界，并探讨了进一步推广到高阶Weil-Oesterlé界的可能性。

Abstract: Weil's theorem gives the most standard bound on the number of points of a
curve over a finite field. This bound was improved by Ihara and Oesterl\'e for
larger genus. Recently, Hallouin and Perret gave a new point of view on these
bounds, that can be obtained by solving a sequence of semi-definite programs,
and the two first steps of this hierarchy recover Weil's and Ihara's bounds. On
the other hand, by taking into account arithmetic constraints, Serre obtained a
refinement on Weil's bound. In this article, we combine these two approaches
and propose a strengthening of Ihara's bound, based on an argument similar to
Serre's refinement. We show that this generically improves upon Ihara's bound,
even in the range where it was the best bound so far. Finally we discuss
possible extensions to higher order Weil-Oesterl\'e bounds.

</details>


### [124] [The non-unit conjecture for Misiurewicz parameters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.05254)
*Robert L. Benedetto,Vefa Goksel*

Main category: math.NT

TL;DR: 研究Misiurewicz参数之间的差是否为代数单位，并在广泛假设下给出新结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Misiurewicz参数在动力模空间中扮演类似奇异模的角色，探索其代数性质。

Method: 基于前期工作，假设不可约性，分析Misiurewicz参数的差。

Result: 在广泛假设下，证明了多个新情况下差不为代数单位。

Conclusion: 动力模空间中的Misiurewicz参数差在特定条件下非代数单位。

Abstract: A Misiurewicz parameter is a complex number $c$ for which the orbit of the
critical point $z=0$ under $z^2+c$ is strictly preperiodic. Such parameters
play the same role in dynamical moduli spaces as singular moduli (corresponding
to CM elliptic curves) play on modular curves. Building on our earlier work, we
investigate whether the difference of two Misiurewicz parameters can be an
algebraic unit. (The corresponding question for singular moduli was recently
answered in the negative by Li.) We answer this dynamical question in many new
cases under a widely believed irreducibility assumption.

</details>

*Toshiki Matsusaka,Miyu Suzuki*

Result: 证明了某些幂级数是模形式，得到了三角数生成函数幂的幂级数恒等式，并揭示了其与仿射李超代数分母恒等式的关系。

Conclusion: 通过扩展不定theta函数理论，论文成功建立了幂级数、模形式与仿射李超代数之间的联系，为相关领域提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We extend the recently developed theory of Roehrig and Zwegers on indefinite
theta functions to prove certain power series are modular forms. As a
consequence, we obtain several power series identities for powers of the
generating function of triangular numbers. We also show that these identities
arise as specializations of denominator identities of affine Lie superalgebras.

### [129] [The Hesse pencil of plane curves and osculating conics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04662)
*Ewelina Nawara*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文重新研究了代数曲线的密切二次曲线和六切点问题，专注于Hesse铅笔的平面三次曲线族，利用射影微分几何工具推导了这些特殊点的显式坐标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用射影微分几何的经典工具，推导密切二次曲线和六切点的显式坐标。

Result: 得到了显式坐标公式，不仅澄清了先前方法，还构建了新的自由和近自由曲线族。

Conclusion: 研究扩展了曲线自由性的理解，并为Hesse铅笔的密切性质提供了新的视角。

Abstract: In this paper, we revisit the classical problem of determining osculating
conics and sextactic points for a given algebraic curve. Our focus is on a
particular family of plane cubic curves known as the Hesse pencil. By employing
classical tools from projective differential geometry, we derive explicit
coordinates for these special points. The resulting formulas not only clarify
previous approaches but also lead to the construction of new families of free
and nearly free curves, extending recent findings the freeness of curves.

### [130] [Intersection of two quadrics: modular interpretation and Hitchin morphism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04707)
*Vladimiro Benedetti,Andreas Höring,Jie Liu*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 论文研究了光滑二次曲面交$X$的余切丛$T^*X$的拉格朗日纤维化，并证明其在$X$作为扭曲Spin-丛模空间时即为Hitchin态射。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨$X$的几何性质及其与Hitchin态射的关系，推广经典结果。

Method: 通过赋予$X$扭曲Spin-丛模空间结构，分析其拉格朗日纤维化与Hitchin态射的对应关系。

Result: 证明了$T^*X$的拉格朗日纤维化即为Hitchin态射，推广了三重情形的经典结果。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了$X$的几何结构与Hitchin态射的深刻联系，为相关领域提供了新的视角。

Abstract: The cotangent bundle $T^*X$ of a smooth intersection $X$ of two quadrics
admits a Lagrangian fibration determined by the intrinsic geometry of $X$. We
show that this fibration is actually the Hitchin morphism if we endow $X$ with
a structure of moduli space of twisted Spin-bundles. This generalises the
classical result for threefolds, in which case it recovers the Hitchin
fibration for the moduli space of rank two bundles with fixed determinant of
odd degree on a curve of genus two.

</details>

### [133] [On the modular cohomology of $GL_2(\mathbb{Z}/p^n)$ and $SL_2(\mathbb{Z}/p^n)$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04720)
*Anja Meyer*

Main category: math.AT

TL;DR: 论文研究了$GL_2(\mathbb{Z}/p^n)$和$SL_2(\mathbb{Z}/p^n)$的Sylow $p$-子群及其扩展群的模$p$上同调，证明了某些扩展群的Lyndon-Hochschild-Serre谱序列的$E_2$页与$n>1$无关，并利用融合系统理论描述了稳定元素的环结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究有限群的模$p$上同调及其Sylow $p$-子群的稳定元素，以理解群上同调的性质。

Method: 利用稳定元素理论和Lyndon-Hochschild-Serre谱序列，分析$GL_2$和$SL_2$的Sylow $p$-子群扩展群的模$p$上同调。

Result: 证明了某些扩展群的谱序列$E_2$页不依赖于$n>1$，并描述了稳定元素的环结构。

Conclusion: 通过融合系统理论，成功描述了稳定元素的环结构，为群上同调的研究提供了新的工具和视角。

Abstract: Let $p$ be an odd prime. Denote a Sylow $p$-subgroup of
$GL_2(\mathbb{Z}/p^n)$ and $SL_2(\mathbb{Z}/p^n)$ by $S_p(n,GL)$ and
$S_p(n,SL)$ respectively. The theory of stable elements tells us that the
mod-$p$ cohomology of a finite group is given by the stable elements of the
mod-$p$ cohomology of it's Sylow $p$-subgroup. We prove that for suitable group
extensions of $S_p(n,GL)$ and $S_p(n,SL)$ the $E_2$-page of the
Lyndon-Hochschild-Serre spectral sequence associated to these extensions does
not depend on $n>1$. Finally, we use the theory of fusion systems to describe
the ring of stable elements.

</details>

### [140] [Remarks on $d$-ary partitions and an application to elementary symmetric partitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04459)

partition, $pre_{j}(\lambda)$, is the partition whose parts are
$\{\lambda_{i_1}\cdots\lambda_{i_j}\;:\;1\leq i_1 < \cdots < i_j\leq \ell\}$.
We prove that if $\lambda$ and $\mu$ are two $d$-ary partitions of length

### [141] [Geodesic transitive graphs of small valency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04670)
*Jun-Jie Huang*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 该论文基于距离传递图的分类，对度数不超过13的测地传递图进行了完整分类，并发现其中有7个图是距离传递但非测地传递的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究测地传递图的分类问题，利用已知的距离传递图分类结果，填补度数不超过13的测地传递图的分类空白。

Method: 利用《Distance-Regular Graphs》中关于度数不超过13的距离传递图的分类结果，进一步分析这些图的测地传递性质。

Result: 完整分类了度数不超过13的测地传递图，并发现其中有7个图是距离传递但非测地传递的。

Conclusion: 论文成功填补了测地传递图分类的空白，为相关研究提供了重要参考。

Abstract: For a graph $\Gamma$, the {\em distance} $d_\Gamma(u,v)$ between two distinct
vertices $u$ and $v$ in $\Gamma$ is defined as the length of the shortest path
from $u$ to $v$, and the {\em diameter} $\mathrm{diam}(\Gamma)$ of $\Gamma$ is
the maximum distance between $u$ and $v$ for all vertices $u$ and $v$ in the
vertex set of $\Gamma$. For a positive integer $s$, a path
$(u_0,u_1,\ldots,u_{s})$ is called an {\em $s$-geodesic} if the distance of
$u_0$ and $u_s$ is $s$. The graph $\Gamma$ is said to be {\em distance
transitive} if for any vertices $u,v,x,y$ of $\Ga$ such that
$d_\Ga(u,v)=d_\Ga(x,y)$, there exists an automorphism of $\Gamma$ that maps the
pair $(u,v)$ to the pair $(x,y)$. Moreover, $\Gamma$ is said to be {\em
geodesic transitive} if for each $i\leq \mathrm{diam}(\Ga)$, the full
automorphism group acts transitively on the set of all $i$-geodesics. In the
monograph [Distance-Regular Graphs, Section 7.5], the authors listed all
distance transitive graphs of valency at most $13$. By using this
classification, in this paper, we provide a complete classification of geodesic
transitive graphs with valency at most $13$. As a result, there are exactly
seven graphs of valency at most $13$ that are distance transitive but not
geodesic transitive.

</details>


### [142] [Spectral Turán problem of non-bipartite graphs: Forbidden books](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04884)
*Ruifang Liu,Lu Miao*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 研究了非二分图$B_{r+1}$-free图的谱Turán问题，证明了其谱半径的上界及极图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受Zhai和Lin关于二分图$B_{r+1}$-free图的谱半径结果的启发，探讨非二分图的情况。

Method: 采用残差指数、Chvátal-Hanson定理和典型谱极值方法。

Result: 证明了非二分图$B_{r+1}$-free图的谱半径上界及其极图。

Conclusion: 发现$r=0$与$r\geq1$时的谱极图完全不同。

Abstract: A book graph $B_{r+1}$ is a set of $r+1$ triangles with a common edge, where
$r\geq0$ is an integer. Zhai and Lin [J. Graph Theory 102 (2023) 502-520]
proved that for $n\geq\frac{13}{2}r$, if $G$ is a $B_{r+1}$-free graph of order
$n$, then $\rho(G)\leq\rho(T_{n,2})$, with equality if and only if $G\cong
T_{n,2}$. Note that the extremal graph $T_{n,2}$ is bipartite. Motivated by the
above elegant result, we investigate the spectral Tur\'{a}n problem of
non-bipartite $B_{r+1}$-free graphs of order $n$. For general $r\geq1$, let
$K_{\lfloor\frac{n-1}{2}\rfloor,\lceil\frac{n-1}{2}\rceil}^{r, r}$ be the graph
obtained from $K_{\lceil\frac{n-1}{2}\rceil,\lfloor\frac{n-1}{2}\rfloor}$ by
adding a new vertex $v_{0}$ such that $v_{0}$ has exactly $r$ neighbours in
each part of $K_{\lceil\frac{n-1}{2}\rceil,\lfloor\frac{n-1}{2}\rfloor}$. By
adopting a different technique named the residual index, Chv\'{a}tal-Hanson
theorem and typical spectral extremal methods, we in this paper prove that: If
$G$ is a non-bipartite $B_{r+1}$-free graph of order $n$, then
$\rho(G)\leq\rho\Big(K_{\lfloor\frac{n-1}{2}\rfloor,\lceil\frac{n-1}{2}\rceil}^{r,
r}\Big)$ , with equality if and only if $G\cong
K_{\lfloor\frac{n-1}{2}\rfloor,\lceil\frac{n-1}{2}\rceil}^{r, r}$. An
interesting phenomenon is that the spectral extremal graphs are completely
different for $r=0$ and general $r\geq1$.

</details>

following problem: given $k \leq d/2$, does the random $d$-regular graph have a
$k$-star decomposition (asymptotically almost surely, provided that the number

has a $k$-star decomposition such that the number of stars centered at each
vertex is either $s$ or $s+1$. Moreover, if $k < d/3$ or $k \leq d/2 - 2.6 \log
d$, we can even prescribe the set of vertices with $s$ stars, as long as it is
of the appropriate size.

Method: 通过定义和证明对称初等分区的唯一性，推导出$d$-ary分区数的新公式。

Result: 证明了若两个$d$-ary分区的对称初等分区相同，则它们本身相同。

Conclusion: 对称初等分区的唯一性为$d$-ary分区的研究提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: We prove new formulas for $p_d(n)$, the number of $d$-ary partitions of $n$,
and, also, for its polynomial part. Given a partition $\lambda
(\lambda_1,\ldots,\lambda_{\ell})$, its associated $j$-th symmetric elementary
partition, $pre_{j}(\lambda)$, is the partition whose parts are
$\{\lambda_{i_1}\cdots\lambda_{i_j}\;:\;1\leq i_1 < \cdots < i_j\leq \ell\}$.
We prove that if $\lambda$ and $\mu$ are two $d$-ary partitions of length
$\ell$ such that $pre_j(\lambda)=pre_j(\mu)$, then $\lambda=\mu$.

### [154] [Geodesic transitive graphs of small valency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04670)
*Jun-Jie Huang*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文基于距离传递图的分类，对度数不超过13的测地传递图进行了完整分类，并发现其中7个图是距离传递但非测地传递的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究测地传递图的分类问题，尤其是度数不超过13的图，以填补现有文献中的空白。

Method: 利用已知的距离传递图分类（度数≤13），通过分析其测地传递性，完成分类。

Result: 完整分类了度数≤13的测地传递图，并发现7个图是距离传递但非测地传递的。

Conclusion: 本文成功分类了度数≤13的测地传递图，为相关领域提供了新的理论支持。

Abstract: For a graph $\Gamma$, the {\em distance} $d_\Gamma(u,v)$ between two distinct
vertices $u$ and $v$ in $\Gamma$ is defined as the length of the shortest path
from $u$ to $v$, and the {\em diameter} $\mathrm{diam}(\Gamma)$ of $\Gamma$ is
the maximum distance between $u$ and $v$ for all vertices $u$ and $v$ in the
vertex set of $\Gamma$. For a positive integer $s$, a path
$(u_0,u_1,\ldots,u_{s})$ is called an {\em $s$-geodesic} if the distance of
$u_0$ and $u_s$ is $s$. The graph $\Gamma$ is said to be {\em distance
transitive} if for any vertices $u,v,x,y$ of $\Ga$ such that
$d_\Ga(u,v)=d_\Ga(x,y)$, there exists an automorphism of $\Gamma$ that maps the
pair $(u,v)$ to the pair $(x,y)$. Moreover, $\Gamma$ is said to be {\em
geodesic transitive} if for each $i\leq \mathrm{diam}(\Ga)$, the full
automorphism group acts transitively on the set of all $i$-geodesics. In the
monograph [Distance-Regular Graphs, Section 7.5], the authors listed all
distance transitive graphs of valency at most $13$. By using this
classification, in this paper, we provide a complete classification of geodesic
transitive graphs with valency at most $13$. As a result, there are exactly
seven graphs of valency at most $13$ that are distance transitive but not
geodesic transitive.

</details>


### [155] [Spectral Turán problem of non-bipartite graphs: Forbidden books](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04884)
*Ruifang Liu,Lu Miao*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 研究了非二部图$B_{r+1}$-free图的谱Turán问题，证明了其谱半径的上界，并确定了极值图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受到Zhai和Lin关于二部图$B_{r+1}$-free图的谱极值结果的启发，探索非二部图情况下的类似问题。

Method: 采用残差指数、Chvátal-Hanson定理和典型谱极值方法，证明了非二部图$B_{r+1}$-free图的谱半径上界。

Result: 证明了非二部图$B_{r+1}$-free图的谱半径不超过$K_{\lfloor\frac{n-1}{2}\rfloor,\lceil\frac{n-1}{2}\rceil}^{r, r}$的谱半径，且极值图唯一。

Conclusion: 发现$r=0$和$r\geq1$时的谱极值图完全不同，为非二部图$B_{r+1}$-free图的谱Turán问题提供了新视角。

Abstract: A book graph $B_{r+1}$ is a set of $r+1$ triangles with a common edge, where
$r\geq0$ is an integer. Zhai and Lin [J. Graph Theory 102 (2023) 502-520]
proved that for $n\geq\frac{13}{2}r$, if $G$ is a $B_{r+1}$-free graph of order
$n$, then $\rho(G)\leq\rho(T_{n,2})$, with equality if and only if $G\cong
T_{n,2}$. Note that the extremal graph $T_{n,2}$ is bipartite. Motivated by the
above elegant result, we investigate the spectral Tur\'{a}n problem of
non-bipartite $B_{r+1}$-free graphs of order $n$. For general $r\geq1$, let
$K_{\lfloor\frac{n-1}{2}\rfloor,\lceil\frac{n-1}{2}\rceil}^{r, r}$ be the graph
obtained from $K_{\lceil\frac{n-1}{2}\rceil,\lfloor\frac{n-1}{2}\rfloor}$ by
adding a new vertex $v_{0}$ such that $v_{0}$ has exactly $r$ neighbours in
each part of $K_{\lceil\frac{n-1}{2}\rceil,\lfloor\frac{n-1}{2}\rfloor}$. By
adopting a different technique named the residual index, Chv\'{a}tal-Hanson
theorem and typical spectral extremal methods, we in this paper prove that: If
$G$ is a non-bipartite $B_{r+1}$-free graph of order $n$, then
$\rho(G)\leq\rho\Big(K_{\lfloor\frac{n-1}{2}\rfloor,\lceil\frac{n-1}{2}\rceil}^{r,
r}\Big)$ , with equality if and only if $G\cong
K_{\lfloor\frac{n-1}{2}\rfloor,\lceil\frac{n-1}{2}\rceil}^{r, r}$. An
interesting phenomenon is that the spectral extremal graphs are completely
different for $r=0$ and general $r\geq1$.

</details>

Abstract: We describe PNim and RNim, two variants of Nim in which piles of tokens are

### [160] [Star decompositions via orientations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.05194)
*Viktor Harangi*

Main category: math.CO

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: A $k$-star decomposition of a graph is a partition of its edges into
$k$-stars (i.e., $k$ edges with a common vertex). The paper studies the
following problem: given $k \leq d/2$, does the random $d$-regular graph have a
$k$-star decomposition (asymptotically almost surely, provided that the number
of edges is divisible by $k$)? Delcourt, Greenhill, Isaev, Lidick\'y, and
Postle proved the a.a.s. existence for every odd $k$ using earlier results
regarding orientations satisfying certain degree conditions modulo $k$.
  In this paper we give a direct, self-contained proof that works for every $d$
and every $k<d/2-1$. In fact, we prove stronger results. Let $s\geq 1$ denote
the integer part of $d/(2k)$. We show that the random $d$-regular graph a.a.s.
has a $k$-star decomposition such that the number of stars centered at each
vertex is either $s$ or $s+1$. Moreover, if $k < d/3$ or $k \leq d/2 - 2.6 \log
d$, we can even prescribe the set of vertices with $s$ stars, as long as it is
of the appropriate size.

### [164] [On the weak and strong Lefschetz properties for initial ideals of determinantal ideals with respect to diagonal monomial orders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.05193)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: Error

Result: Error

Abstract: We study the weak and strong Lefschetz properties for $R/\mathrm{in}(I_t)$,
where $I_t$ is the ideal of a polynomial ring $R$ generated by the $t$-minors
of an $m\times n$ matrix of indeterminates, and $\mathrm{in}(I_t)$ denotes the
initial ideal of $I_t$ with respect to a diagonal monomial order. We show that
when $I_t$ is generated by maximal minors (that is, $t=\mathrm{min}\{m,n\}$),

$R/\mathrm{in}(I_t)$ fails to satisfy the weak Lefschetz property whenever the
product $mn$ exceeds this bound. As an application, we present counterexamples
that provide a negative answer to a question posed by Murai regarding the
preservation of Lefschetz properties under square-free Gr\"obner degenerations.

the ring $R/\mathrm{in}(I_t)$ has the strong Lefschetz property for all $m$,
$n$. In contrast, for $t<\mathrm{min}\{m,n\}$, we provide a bound such that
$R/\mathrm{in}(I_t)$ fails to satisfy the weak Lefschetz property whenever the
product $mn$ exceeds this bound. As an application, we present counterexamples
that provide a negative answer to a question posed by Murai regarding the
preservation of Lefschetz properties under square-free Gr\"obner degenerations.

</details>

$\{I_n\}_{n\geqslant 0}$ of $\mathfrak{m}_R$-primary ideals such that the union
of all the sets of Rees valuations of all the $I_n$ is a finite set, and
another example of a (necessarily non-Noetherian) divisorial filtration of

### [169] [Cauchy Integral, Fractional Sobolev Spaces and Chord-Arc Curves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04564)
*Huaying Wei,Michel Zinsmeister*

Main category: math.CV

TL;DR: 论文研究了有界Jordan曲线Γ上定义的两种函数空间H^s(Γ)和H^s(Γ)的等价性，并探讨了其在Lipschitz曲线上的成立条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究不同曲线条件下两种函数空间的等价性，特别是针对Lipschitz曲线的特殊情况。

Method: 通过定义和分析两种函数空间的性质，结合调和扩展和可积性条件，探讨其等价性。

Result: 证明了在Lipschitz曲线上，两种空间H^s(Γ)和H^s(Γ)是等价的。

Conclusion: 为曲线上的函数空间理论提供了新的见解，特别是在Lipschitz曲线上的应用。

Abstract: Let $\Gamma$ be a bounded Jordan curve and $\Omega_i,\Omega_e$ its two
complementary components. For $s\in(0,1)$ we define $\mathcal{H}^s(\Gamma)$ as
the set of functions $f:\Gamma\to \mathbb C$ having harmonic extension $u$ in
$\Omega_i\cup \Omega_e$ such that $$ \iint_{\Omega_i\cup \Omega_e} |\nabla
u(z)|^2 d(z,\Gamma)^{1-2s} dxdy<+\infty.$$ If $\Gamma$ is further assumed to be
rectifiable we define $H^s(\Gamma)$ as the space of measurable functions
$f:\Gamma\to \mathbb C$ such that $$\iint_{\Gamma\times
\Gamma}\frac{|f(z)-f(\zeta)|^2}{|z-\zeta|^{1+2s}}
d\sigma(z)d\sigma(\zeta)<+\infty.$$ When $\Gamma$ is the unit circle these two
spaces coincide with the homogeneous fractional Sobolev space defined via
Fourier series. For a general rectifiable curve these two spaces need not
coincide and our first goal is to investigate the cases of equality: while the
chord-arc property is the necessary and sufficient condition for equality in
the classical case of $s=1/2$, this is no longer the case for general $s\in
(0,1)$. We show however that equality holds for Lipschitz curves.
  The second goal involves the Plemelj-Calder\'on problem. ......

</details>


### [170] [Note on real and imaginary parts of harmonic quasiregular mappings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04618)
*Suman Das,Antti Rasila*

Main category: math.CV

TL;DR: 论文证明了在单位圆盘中，若复值调和函数是K-拟正则的，其实部和虚部的积分均值具有相同的增长阶，并进一步展示了其实部和虚部在边界上的光滑度相同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究复值调和函数在拟正则条件下的积分均值增长阶和边界光滑度的关系，扩展了近期关于调和拟正则映射的Riesz型定理。

Method: 假设复值调和函数是K-拟正则的，分析其实部和虚部的积分均值增长阶及边界光滑度。

Result: 证明了在K-拟正则条件下，调和函数的实部和虚部的积分均值增长阶相同，且边界光滑度一致。

Conclusion: 该研究为调和拟正则映射的性质提供了新的理论支持，扩展了相关领域的研究成果。

Abstract: If $f=u+iv$ is analytic in the unit disk $\mathbb{D}$, it is known that the
integral means $M_p(r,u)$ and $M_p(r,v)$ have the same order of growth. This is
false if $f$ is a (complex-valued) harmonic function. However, we prove that
the same principle holds if we assume, in addition, that $f$ is
$K$-quasiregular in $\mathbb{D}$. The case $0<p<1$ is particularly interesting,
and is an extension of the recent Riesz type theorems for harmonic quasiregular
mappings by several authors. Further, we proceed to show that the real and
imaginary parts of a harmonic quasiregular mapping have the same degree of
smoothness on the boundary.

</details>

problems and minimization involving of polar integral Legendre polynomials.

### [176] [On the geometry of synthetic null hypersurfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04934)
*Fabio Cavalletti,Davide Manini,Andrea Mondino*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个合成框架，用于研究非光滑时空中的零（光状）超曲面，定义了合成零能量条件，并证明了其在低正则性时空中的稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将经典微分几何结构推广到可能奇异的时空，为低正则性时空提供几何和分析工具。

Method: 通过最优传输和洛伦兹几何的进展，定义合成零超曲面为三元组$(H, G, \mathfrak{m})$，并引入合成零能量条件$\mathsf{NC}^e(N)$。

Result: 证明了合成零能量条件的稳定性，并推广了霍金面积定理和彭罗斯奇点定理到连续时空和拓扑因果空间。

Conclusion: 该框架为研究非光滑时空中的零超曲面提供了新工具，并扩展了经典结果的应用范围。

Abstract: This paper develops a synthetic framework for the geometric and analytic
study of null (lightlike) hypersurfaces in non-smooth spacetimes. Drawing from
optimal transport and recent advances in Lorentzian geometry and causality
theory, we define a synthetic null hypersurface as a triple $(H, G,
\mathfrak{m})$: $H$ is a closed achronal set in a topological causal space, $G$
is a gauge function encoding affine parametrizations along null generators, and
$\mathfrak{m}$ is a Radon measure serving as a synthetic analog of the rigged
measure. This generalizes classical differential geometric structures to
potentially singular spacetimes.
  A central object is the synthetic null energy condition ($\mathsf{NC}^e(N)$),
defined via the concavity of an entropy power functional along optimal
transport, with parametrization given by the gauge $G$. This condition is
invariant under changes of gauge and measure within natural equivalence
classes. It agrees with the classical Null Energy Condition in the smooth
setting and it applies to low-regularity spacetimes. A key property of
$\mathsf{NC}^e(N)$ is the stability under convergence of synthetic null
hypersurfaces, inspired by measured Gromov--Hausdorff convergence.
  As a first application, we obtain a synthetic version of Hawking's area
theorem. Moreover, we obtain various sharpenings of the celebrated Penrose's
singularity theorem: for smooth spacetimes we show that the incomplete null
geodesic whose existence is guaranteed by Penrose's argument is actually
maximizing; we extend Penrose's singularity theorem to continuous spacetimes;
we prove the existence of trapped regions in the general setting of topological
causal spaces satisfying the synthetic $\mathsf{NC}^e(N)$.

</details>

### [178] [The asymptotics of the $\mathrm{SL}_2(\mathbb{C})$-Hitchin metric on the singular locus: subintegrable systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04957)

Abstract: We study the asymptotic hyperk\"ahler geometry of the
$\mathrm{SL}_2(\mathbb{C})$-Hitchin moduli space over the singular fibers of
the Hitchin fibration. We extend the previously known exponential convergence
results for solutions to the Hitchin equation to the class of locally fiducial
Higgs bundles defined by a special local description at the singularities of

exponentially fast to the corresponding semi-flat metric along a ray

for each stratum of quadratic differentials there is a closed subset of the

### [179] [Minimizing the Gauss map area of surfaces in $\mathbb{S}^3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.05141)
*Gerard Orriols,Tristan Rivière*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 论文证明了闭合定向曲面在S³中的浸入的高斯映射面积的下界为4π(1+g)，并描述了极小化序列的行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究高斯映射面积的下界及其在极小化序列中的行为，为Willmore猜想提供理论基础。

Method: 通过分析高斯映射的积分循环和曲率集中现象，证明了面积下界及其最优性。

Result: 下界4π(1+g)对任何g∈ℕ最优，但仅当g=0时可达；极小化序列收敛于圆球面，高斯映射的积分循环分裂为g+1个球面。

Conclusion: 结果为第二作者定义非平凡同调4维极小极大方案提供了基础，与Willmore猜想相关。

Abstract: We establish the lower bound of $4\pi(1+g)$ for the area of the Gauss map of
any immersion of a closed oriented surface of genus $g$ into $\mathbb{S}^3$,
taking values in the Grassmannian of $2$-planes in $\mathbb{R}^4$. This lower
bound is proved to be optimal for any genus $g \in \mathbb{N}$ but attained
only when $g = 0$. For $g \neq 0$ we describe the behavior of any minimizing
sequence of embeddings: we prove that, modulo extraction of a subsequence, the
surfaces converge in the Hausdorff distance to a round sphere $S$, and the
integral cycles carried by the Gauss maps split into $g+1$ spheres, each of
area $4\pi$; one of them corresponds to the cycle carried by the Gauss map of
$S$, while the other $g$ arise from the concentration of negative Gauss
curvature at $g$ points of $S$.
  The results of this paper are used by the second author to define a
nontrivial homological 4-dimensional min-max scheme for the area of Gauss maps
of immersions into $\mathbb{S}^3$ in relation to the Willmore conjecture.

</details>

Method: 通过定义一个三元组（H, G, m）作为合成零超曲面，结合最优传输和熵功率泛函的凹性，提出合成零能量条件（NC^e(N)）。

Conclusion: 该框架为研究低正则性时空中的零超曲面提供了新工具，并扩展了经典定理的应用范围。

Abstract: This paper develops a synthetic framework for the geometric and analytic
study of null (lightlike) hypersurfaces in non-smooth spacetimes. Drawing from
optimal transport and recent advances in Lorentzian geometry and causality
theory, we define a synthetic null hypersurface as a triple $(H, G,
\mathfrak{m})$: $H$ is a closed achronal set in a topological causal space, $G$
is a gauge function encoding affine parametrizations along null generators, and
$\mathfrak{m}$ is a Radon measure serving as a synthetic analog of the rigged
measure. This generalizes classical differential geometric structures to
potentially singular spacetimes.
  A central object is the synthetic null energy condition ($\mathsf{NC}^e(N)$),
defined via the concavity of an entropy power functional along optimal
transport, with parametrization given by the gauge $G$. This condition is
invariant under changes of gauge and measure within natural equivalence
classes. It agrees with the classical Null Energy Condition in the smooth
setting and it applies to low-regularity spacetimes. A key property of
$\mathsf{NC}^e(N)$ is the stability under convergence of synthetic null
hypersurfaces, inspired by measured Gromov--Hausdorff convergence.
  As a first application, we obtain a synthetic version of Hawking's area
theorem. Moreover, we obtain various sharpenings of the celebrated Penrose's
singularity theorem: for smooth spacetimes we show that the incomplete null
geodesic whose existence is guaranteed by Penrose's argument is actually
maximizing; we extend Penrose's singularity theorem to continuous spacetimes;
we prove the existence of trapped regions in the general setting of topological
causal spaces satisfying the synthetic $\mathsf{NC}^e(N)$.

</details>

*Juanling Lu,Yu Zheng*

### [183] [The asymptotics of the $\mathrm{SL}_2(\mathbb{C})$-Hitchin metric on the singular locus: subintegrable systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04957)

Abstract: We study the asymptotic hyperk\"ahler geometry of the
$\mathrm{SL}_2(\mathbb{C})$-Hitchin moduli space over the singular fibers of
the Hitchin fibration. We extend the previously known exponential convergence
results for solutions to the Hitchin equation to the class of locally fiducial

### [184] [Minimizing the Gauss map area of surfaces in $\mathbb{S}^3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.05141)
*Gerard Orriols,Tristan Rivière*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 论文证明了闭合定向曲面在$\mathbb{S}^3$中的浸入的高斯映射面积的下界为$4\pi(1+g)$，并描述了极小化序列的行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究高斯映射面积的下界及其极小化序列的性质，为后续的Willmore猜想相关研究提供理论基础。

Method: 通过分析高斯映射的积分循环和曲率集中现象，证明下界并描述极小化序列的收敛行为。

Result: 下界$4\pi(1+g)$对任意$g$最优，但仅在$g=0$时可达；极小化序列收敛到一个球面，高斯映射的积分循环分裂为$g+1$个球面。

Conclusion: 结果为后续的高维极小化方案提供了基础，尤其是与Willmore猜想相关的同调理论。

Abstract: We establish the lower bound of $4\pi(1+g)$ for the area of the Gauss map of
any immersion of a closed oriented surface of genus $g$ into $\mathbb{S}^3$,
taking values in the Grassmannian of $2$-planes in $\mathbb{R}^4$. This lower
bound is proved to be optimal for any genus $g \in \mathbb{N}$ but attained
only when $g = 0$. For $g \neq 0$ we describe the behavior of any minimizing
sequence of embeddings: we prove that, modulo extraction of a subsequence, the
surfaces converge in the Hausdorff distance to a round sphere $S$, and the
integral cycles carried by the Gauss maps split into $g+1$ spheres, each of
area $4\pi$; one of them corresponds to the cycle carried by the Gauss map of
$S$, while the other $g$ arise from the concentration of negative Gauss
curvature at $g$ points of $S$.
  The results of this paper are used by the second author to define a
nontrivial homological 4-dimensional min-max scheme for the area of Gauss maps
of immersions into $\mathbb{S}^3$ in relation to the Willmore conjecture.

</details>

### [185] [Profiles of Critical Flat Ribbon Knots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04403)
*José Ayala*

Main category: math.GT

TL;DR: 本文计算了几种著名结图的最小带长，包括Salomon结和Turk's head结，并提出了将带长与结不变量关联的猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管经过几十年的密集研究，关于理想结的示例仍然稀缺。本文旨在填补这一空白，通过计算最小带长为结的分类提供新视角。

Method: 使用直接方法计算了granny结和square结的最小带长，并确定了无限类临界带结的带长。

Result: 确定了Salomon结、Turk's head结、granny结和square结的最小带长，并提出了带长与结不变量关联的猜想。

Conclusion: 本文为结的度量分类提供了新工具，并提出了进一步研究的猜想。

Abstract: The main open problem in geometric knot theory is to provide a tabulation of
knots based on an energy criterion, with the goal of presenting this tabulation
in terms of global energy minimisers within isotopy classes, often referred to
as ideal knots. Recently, the first examples of minimal length diagrams and
their corresponding length values have been determined by Ayala, Kirszenblat,
and Rubinstein. This article is motivated by the scarcity of examples despite
several decades of intense research. Here, we compute the minimal ribbonlength
for some well-known knot diagrams, including the Salomon knot and the Turk's
head knot. We also determine the minimal ribbonlength for the granny knot and

relating ribbonlength to knot invariants in pursuit of a metric classification
of knots.

*Luc Ta*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We solve two open problems of Valeriy Bardakov about Cayley graphs of racks

  First, we characterize markings of graphs that realize racks. As an

  Second, we show that all right quasigroups are realizable by edgeless graphs

### [187] [Geometric Constraints in Link Isotopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04442)
*José Ayala*

Main category: math.GT

TL;DR: 论文证明了物理无结的多种同痕类的存在性，通过参数化厚度的概念，这些无结具有特定长度、管厚度和曲率限制，且无法通过保持约束的同痕解为加厚圆环。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究几何约束下无结的复杂性，验证长期猜想的存在性。

Method: 利用参数化厚度和几何约束（曲率、自距离）分析无结的同痕类。

Result: 发现几何锁定的无结（Gordian unknots），揭示了无限多不连通的分层结构。

Conclusion: 几何约束在拓扑平凡构型中引入了丰富的层次化纠缠结构。

Abstract: We prove the existence of families of distinct isotopy classes of physical
unknots through the key concept of parametrised thickness. These unknots have
prescribed length, tube thickness, a uniform bound on curvature, and cannot be
disentangled into a thickened round circle by an isotopy that preserves these
constraints throughout. In particular, we establish the existence of
\emph{gordian unknots}: embedded tubes that are topologically trivial but
geometrically locked, confirming a long-standing conjecture. These arise within
the space $\mathcal{U}_1$ of thin unknots in $\mathbb{R}^3$, and persist across
a stratified family $\{ \mathcal{U}_\tau \}_{\tau \in [0,2]}$, where $\tau$
denotes the tube diameter, or thickness. The constraints on curvature and
self-distance fragment the isotopy class of the unknot into infinitely many
disconnected components, revealing a stratified structure governed by geometric
thresholds. This unveils a rich hierarchy of geometric entanglement within
topologically trivial configurations.

</details>


### [188] [Gordian split links in the Gehring ropelength problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04644)
*Friedrich Bauermeister*

Main category: math.GT

TL;DR: 论文研究了厚链接和厚嵌入链接的概念，构造了无法通过厚同伦分裂的厚嵌入4分量链接，并首次明确构造了绳索长度的非全局局部最小值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索厚链接和厚嵌入链接的性质，解决Gehring绳索长度问题，并研究厚同伦和厚同痕的限制。

Method: 定义厚链接和厚嵌入链接，构造具体例子，分析其性质，并通过厚同伦和厚同痕验证其不可分裂性。

Result: 构造了无法通过厚同伦分裂的厚嵌入4分量链接，以及绳索长度的非全局局部最小值的2分量链接。

Conclusion: 厚同伦和厚同痕的限制性更强，首次明确构造了非全局局部最小值的绳索长度例子。

Abstract: A thick link is a link in Euclidean three-space such that each component of
the link lies at distance at least 1 from every other component. Strengthening
the notion of thickness, we define a thickly embedded link to be a thick link
whose open radius-1/2 normal disk bundles of all components are embedded. The
Gehring ropelength problem asks how large the sum of the lengths of the
components of a thick (respectively thickly embedded) link must be, given the
link homotopy (respectively isotopy) class of the link. A thick homotopy
(isotopy) is a link homotopy (isotopy) of a thick (thickly embedded) link that
preserves thickness throughout, and such that during the homotopy the total
length of the link never exceeds the initial total length. These notions of
thick homotopy and isotopy are more permissive than other notions of physical
link isotopies in which the length of each individual component must remain
constant (no "length trading"). We construct an explicit example of a thickly
embedded 4-component link which is topologically split but cannot be split by a
thick homotopy, and thick links in every homotopy class with 2 components that
are non-global local minima for ropelength. This is the first time such local
minima for ropelength have been explicitly constructed. In particular, we
construct a thick 2-component link in the link homotopy class of the unlink
which cannot be split through a thick homotopy.

</details>

*Hanwool Bae,Cheol-Hyun Cho,Dongwook Choa,Wonbo Jeong,Pablo Portilla Cuadrado*

Conclusion: 几何变分算子和消失弧集为理解奇点拓扑提供了新工具，扩展了经典框架的应用范围。

Abstract: The variation operator associated with an isolated hypersurface singularity
is a classical topological invariant that relates relative and absolute
homologies of the Milnor fiber via a non trivial isomorphism. Here we work with
a topological version of this operator that deals with proper arcs and closed
curves instead of homology cycles. Building on the classical framework of
geometric vanishing cycles, we introduce the concept of vanishing arcsets as
their counterpart using this geometric variation operator. We characterize
which properly embedded arcs are sent to geometric vanishing cycles by the
geometric variation operator in terms of intersections numbers of the arcs and
their images by the geometric monodromy. Furthermore, we prove that for any
distinguished collection of vanishing cycles arising from an A'Campo's divide,
there exists a topological exceptional collection of arcsets whose variation
images match this collection.

constant (no "length trading"). We construct an explicit example of a thickly
embedded 4-component link which is topologically split but cannot be split by a
thick homotopy, and thick links in every homotopy class with 2 components that
are non-global local minima for ropelength. This is the first time such local
minima for ropelength have been explicitly constructed. In particular, we
construct a thick 2-component link in the link homotopy class of the unlink
which cannot be split through a thick homotopy.

</details>


### [195] [Vanishing arcs for isolated plane curve singularities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04917)
*Hanwool Bae,Cheol-Hyun Cho,Dongwook Choa,Wonbo Jeong,Pablo Portilla Cuadrado*

Main category: math.GT

TL;DR: 论文研究了孤立超曲面奇点的几何变分算子，引入消失弧集概念，并证明了其与几何消失循环的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索几何变分算子在拓扑版本中的作用，特别是如何通过几何消失循环的框架理解弧集的性质。

Method: 利用几何变分算子和几何单值性，分析弧集与消失循环的交点数量关系，并构建拓扑例外弧集。

Result: 证明了弧集通过几何变分算子映射为几何消失循环的条件，并构建了与A'Campo分割匹配的拓扑例外弧集。

Conclusion: 几何变分算子在弧集与消失循环之间建立了有效联系，为拓扑研究提供了新工具。

Abstract: The variation operator associated with an isolated hypersurface singularity
is a classical topological invariant that relates relative and absolute
homologies of the Milnor fiber via a non trivial isomorphism. Here we work with
a topological version of this operator that deals with proper arcs and closed
curves instead of homology cycles. Building on the classical framework of
geometric vanishing cycles, we introduce the concept of vanishing arcsets as
their counterpart using this geometric variation operator. We characterize
which properly embedded arcs are sent to geometric vanishing cycles by the
geometric variation operator in terms of intersections numbers of the arcs and
their images by the geometric monodromy. Furthermore, we prove that for any
distinguished collection of vanishing cycles arising from an A'Campo's divide,
there exists a topological exceptional collection of arcsets whose variation
images match this collection.

</details>


### [196] [Characterization of Infinite Ideal Polyhedra in Hyperbolic 3-Space via Combinatorial Ricci Flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.05036)

Conclusion: 组合Ricci流为无限理想多面体的表征提供了有效工具，解决了长期未决的问题。

Abstract: In his seminal work \cite{Ri96}, Rivin characterized finite ideal polyhedra

infinite ideal polyhedra, as proposed by Rivin, has remained a long-standing

infinite ideal circle patterns, a discrete analogue of Ricci flow on
non-compact Riemannian manifolds, and prove a characterization of such circle
patterns under certain combinatorial conditions. Our results provide
affirmative solutions to Rivin's problem.

### [197] [Proper actions on finite products of hyperbolic spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04856)
*Bingxue Tao,Renxing Wan*

Main category: math.GR

TL;DR: 本文研究了群的性质（PH'）和（PH），并给出了从线性作用出发的完整刻画。同时，通过群的中心扩张，证明了（PH）和（QT）的等价性，并推广到直积和图形积群。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了推广Bestvina-Bromberg-Fujiwara提出的性质（QT），本文引入了性质（PH'）和（PH），旨在更广泛地研究群在双曲空间上的作用。

Method: 通过群的中心扩张、直积和图形积群的结构，分析性质（PH）和（QT）的等价性及其条件。

Result: 证明了群E具有性质（PH）或（QT）当且仅当G具有相应性质且扩张的欧拉类有界。此外，刻画了3-流形群的性质（PH），并给出了更多具有（QT）的群例子。

Conclusion: 性质（PH）和（QT）在中心扩张、直积和图形积群中具有明确的等价条件，为群作用的研究提供了新的工具和例子。

Abstract: A group $G$ is said to have property (PH') if there exist finitely many
hyperbolic spaces $X_1,\cdots,X_n$ on which $G$ acts coboundedly such that the
diagonal action of $G$ on the product $\prod_{i=1}^nX_i$ equipped with
$\ell^1$-metric is proper. A group $G$ has property (PH) if it virtually has
property (PH'). This notion is a generalization of property (QT) introduced by
Bestvina-Bromberg-Fujiwara \cite{BBF21}. In this paper, we initiate the study
of property (PH) of groups and give a complete characterization of groups with
property (PH') or (PH) from lineal actions.
  In addition, by considering a central extension of groups $1\to Z\to E\to
G\to 1$, we prove that $E$ has property (PH) (resp. (QT)) if and only if $G$
has property (PH) (resp. (QT)) and the Euler class of the extension is bounded.
We also derive similar results for amalgamated direct products and graph
products. As corollaries, we characterize when 3-manifold groups have property
(PH) and obtain more interesting examples with property (QT) including the
central extension of residually finite hyperbolic groups, the mapping class
group of any finite-type surface and the outer automorphism group of
torsion-free one-ended hyperbolic groups.

</details>


### [198] [On some semidirect products of skew braces arising in Hopf-Galois theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04928)
*Paul J. Truman*

Main category: math.GR

TL;DR: 分类斜撑结构为理想与左理想的半直积，并应用于Galois扩张的Hopf-Galois结构分类，研究其代数性质与局部域扩展的积分模结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究斜撑结构与Galois扩张的Hopf-Galois结构之间的关系，以解决代数扩张中的结构问题。

Method: 分类斜撑结构的半直积形式，并应用于Galois扩张的Hopf-Galois结构，通过Hopf子代数的直积描述。

Result: 证明了Hopf-Galois结构的Hopf代数是Hopf子代数的直积，并研究了广义正规基生成器和局部域扩展的积分模结构。

Conclusion: 通过斜撑结构的分类，为Galois扩张的Hopf-Galois结构提供了新的描述工具，并扩展了其在局部域中的应用。

Abstract: We classify skew braces that are the semidirect product of an ideal and a
left ideal. As a consequence, given a Galois extension of fields $ L/K $ whose
Galois group is the semidirect product of a normal subgroup $ A $ and a
subgroup $ B $, we classify the Hopf-Galois structures on $ L/K $ that realize
$ L^{A} $ via a normal Hopf subalgebra and $ L^{B} $ via a Hopf subalgebra. We
show that the Hopf algebra giving such a Hopf-Galois structure is the smash
product of these Hopf subalgebras, and use this description to study
generalized normal basis generators and questions of integral module structure
in extensions of local fields.

</details>


### [199] [Hausdorff Dimension of non-conical and Myrberg limit sets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04955)
*Mahan Mj,Wenyuan Yang*

Main category: math.GR

TL;DR: 研究了负曲率空间中群作用的非锥形和Myrberg极限集的Hausdorff维数，证明了非锥形极限集维数在某些情况下的极大性，并验证了Myrberg极限集维数与临界指数相同的猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨负曲率空间中群作用的极限集性质，特别是非锥形和Myrberg极限集的Hausdorff维数，以验证相关猜想并扩展理论结果。

Method: 针对不同几何结构（如有限体积黎曼流形、规则树、双曲平面等），分析群作用下的极限集维数，并证明其极大性。

Result: 在四种情况下证明了非锥形极限集维数的极大性，并确认Myrberg极限集维数与临界指数相同。

Conclusion: 研究扩展了对负曲率空间中群作用极限集的理解，验证了Falk-Matsuzaki猜想，为相关领域提供了新的理论支持。

Abstract: In this paper, we develop techniques to study the Hausdorff dimensions of
non-conical and Myrberg limit sets for groups acting on negatively curved
spaces. We establish maximality of the Hausdorff dimension of the non-conical
limit set of $G$ in the following cases. 1. $M$ is a finite volume complete
Riemannian manifold of pinched negative curvature and $G$ is an infinite normal
subgroups of infinite index in $\pi_1(M)$. 2. $G$ acts on a regular tree $X$
with $X/G$ infinite and amenable (dimension 1). 3. $G$ acts on the hyperbolic
plane $\mathbb H^2$ such that $\mathbb H^2/G$ has Cheeger constant zero
(dimension 2). 4. $G$ is a finitely generated geometrically infinite Kleinian
group (dimension 3). We also show that the Hausdorff dimension of the Myrberg
limit set is the same as the critical exponent, confirming a conjecture of
Falk-Matsuzaki.

### [205] [Polarized 6D Movable Antenna for Wireless Communication: Channel Modeling and Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04471)
*Xiaodan Shao,Qijun Jiang,Derrick Wing Kwan Ng,Naofal Al-Dhahir*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 提出了一种新型极化六维可移动天线（P-6DMA），通过电调极化和机械旋转天线，结合极化和空间多样性优化无线通信性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通过极化和空间多样性重新配置无线信道，提升通信性能。

Method: 建模P-6DMA信道，提出两时间尺度传输协议，优化天线旋转和极化向量设计，采用低复杂度算法解决联合设计问题。

Result: 仿真结果显示极化、天线旋转及其联合设计显著优于未优化的基准方案。

Abstract: In this paper, we propose a novel polarized six-dimensional movable antenna
(P-6DMA) to enhance the performance of wireless communication cost-effectively.
Specifically, the P-6DMA enables polarforming by adaptively tuning the
antenna's polarization electrically as well as controls the antenna's rotation
mechanically, thereby exploiting both polarization and spatial diversity to
reconfigure wireless channels for improving communication performance. First,
we model the P-6DMA channel in terms of transceiver antenna polarforming
vectors and antenna rotations. We then propose a new two-timescale transmission
protocol to maximize the weighted sum-rate for a P-6DMA-enhanced multiuser
system. Specifically, antenna rotations at the base station (BS) are first
optimized based on the statistical channel state information (CSI) of all
users, which varies at a much slower rate compared to their instantaneous CSI.
Then, transceiver polarforming vectors are designed to cater to the
instantaneous CSI under the optimized BS antennas' rotations. Under the
polarforming phase shift and amplitude constraints, a new polarforming and
rotation joint design problem is efficiently addressed by a low-complexity
algorithm based on penalty dual decomposition, where the polarforming
coefficients are updated in parallel to reduce computational time. Simulation
results demonstrate the significant performance advantages of polarforming,
antenna rotation, and their joint design in comparison with various benchmarks
without polarforming or antenna rotation adaptation.

</details>


### [206] [Sparse Phase Retrieval with Redundant Dictionary via $\ell_q (0<q\le 1)$-Analysis Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04576)

Abstract: Sparse phase retrieval with redundant dictionary is to reconstruct the
signals of interest that are (nearly) sparse in a redundant dictionary or frame
from the phaseless measurements via the optimization models. Gao [7] presented
conditions on the measurement matrix, called null space property (NSP) and
strong dictionary restricted isometry property (S-DRIP), for exact and stable
recovery of dictionary-$k$-sparse signals via the $\ell_1$-analysis model for
sparse phase retrieval with redundant dictionary, respectively, where, in
particularly, the S-DRIP of order $tk$ with $t>1$ was derived. In this paper,
motivated by many advantages of the $\ell_q$ minimization with $0<q\leq1$,
e.g., reduction of the number of measurements required, we generalize these two
conditions to the $\ell_q$-analysis model. Specifically, we first present two
NSP variants for exact recovery of dictionary-$k$-sparse signals via the
$\ell_q$-analysis model in the noiseless scenario. Moreover, we investigate the

Motivation: 物联网设备通过随机接入协议（如ALOHA）传输时间戳更新，但碰撞解决算法的性能对数据新鲜度（AoI）有重要影响。本文旨在首次分析Capetanakis树算法在门控访问下的平均AoI。

Method: 采用Capetanakis树算法，分析其在门控访问和早期终止变体中的性能，捕捉协议动态（如零星数据包生成和可变碰撞解决时间）。

Result: 研究发现，早期终止变体在可靠性和时效性之间存在权衡，允许丢弃过时数据包以提高新鲜度。

Abstract: Age of Information (AoI) has emerged as a key metric for assessing data
freshness in IoT applications, where a large number of devices report
time-stamped updates to a monitor. Such systems often rely on random access
protocols based on variations of ALOHA at the link layer, where collision
resolution algorithms play a fundamental role to enable reliable delivery of
packets. In this context, we provide the first analytical characterization of
average AoI for the classical Capetanakis tree-based algorithm with gated

stale packets to be dropped to improve freshness.

### [209] [Iterative Neural Rollback Chase-Pyndiah Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04839)
*Dmitry Artemasov,Oleg Nesterenkov,Kirill Andreev,Pavel Rybin,Alexey Frolov*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 论文提出了一种基于神经网络的回滚Chase-Pyndiah解码方法，通过Transformer神经网络识别可能导致错误的外在信息更新，从而提升解码性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在迭代解码中，初始迭代时组件码表现不佳，引入错误的外在信息更新，限制了TPC的性能。

Method: 使用Transformer神经网络识别潜在的错误外在更新，触发回滚机制以避免更新。

Result: 实验表明，该方法在TPC方案中显著提升了解码性能，比传统方法增益约0.145 dB。

Conclusion: 神经网络辅助的回滚机制有效解决了外在信息更新中的错误问题，提升了TPC的解码性能。

Abstract: Iterative decoding is essential in modern communication systems, especially
optical communications, where error-correcting codes such as turbo product
codes (TPC) and staircase codes are widely employed. A key factor in achieving
high error correction performance is the use of soft-decision decoding for
component codes. However, implementing optimal maximum a posteriori (MAP)
probability decoding for commonly used component codes, such as BCH and Polar
codes, is computationally prohibitive. Instead, practical systems rely on
approximations, with the Chase-Pyndiah algorithm being a widely used suboptimal
method. TPC are more powerful than their component codes and begin to function
effectively at low signal-to-noise ratios. Consequently, during the initial
iterations, the component codes do not perform well and introduce errors in the
extrinsic information updates. This phenomenon limits the performance of TPC.
This paper proposes a neural network-aided rollback Chase-Pyndiah decoding
method to address this issue. A transformer-based neural network identifies
cases where extrinsic updates are likely to introduce errors, triggering a
rollback mechanism which prevents the update and keeps the component code
message intact. Our results demonstrate that a neural network with a relatively
small number of parameters can effectively distinguish destructive updates and
improve decoding performance. We evaluate the proposed approach using TPC with
(256, 239) extended BCH component codes. We show that the proposed method
enhances the bit error rate performance of Chase-Pyndiah p=6 decoding,
achieving a gain of approximately 0.145 dB in a TPC scheme with four full
iterations, significantly outperforming conventional Chase p=7 decoding.

</details>

Abstract: The problem of resource allocation in goal-oriented semantic communication
with semantic-aware utilities and subjective risk perception is studied here.
By linking information importance to risk aversion, we model agent behavior
using Cumulative Prospect Theory (CPT), which incorporates risk-sensitive
utility functions and nonlinear transformations of distributions, reflecting
subjective perceptions of gains and losses. The objective is to maximize the
aggregate utility across multiple CPT-modeled agents, which leads to a
nonconvex, nonsmooth optimization problem. To efficiently solve this
challenging problem, we propose a new algorithmic framework that combines

Lagrangian relaxation, Our approach enables tractable optimization while
preserving solution quality, offering both theoretical rigor and practical
effectiveness in semantics-aware resource allocation.

information, avoiding the need for full CSI transmission or reconstruction

(P-6DMA) to enhance the performance of wireless communication cost-effectively.
Specifically, the P-6DMA enables polarforming by adaptively tuning the
antenna's polarization electrically as well as controls the antenna's rotation
mechanically, thereby exploiting both polarization and spatial diversity to
reconfigure wireless channels for improving communication performance. First,
we model the P-6DMA channel in terms of transceiver antenna polarforming
vectors and antenna rotations. We then propose a new two-timescale transmission
protocol to maximize the weighted sum-rate for a P-6DMA-enhanced multiuser

instantaneous CSI under the optimized BS antennas' rotations. Under the
polarforming phase shift and amplitude constraints, a new polarforming and
rotation joint design problem is efficiently addressed by a low-complexity
algorithm based on penalty dual decomposition, where the polarforming
coefficients are updated in parallel to reduce computational time. Simulation
results demonstrate the significant performance advantages of polarforming,
antenna rotation, and their joint design in comparison with various benchmarks
without polarforming or antenna rotation adaptation.

### [219] [Optimization for Semantic-Aware Resource Allocation under CPT-based Utilities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04952)
*Symeon Vaidanis,Photios A. Stavrou,Marios Kountouris*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 研究了基于语义感知效用和主观风险感知的目标导向语义通信中的资源分配问题，提出了一种结合CPT理论和SCA算法的新框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决语义通信中资源分配的复杂性和主观风险感知问题，优化多代理系统的聚合效用。

Method: 使用累积前景理论（CPT）建模代理行为，结合SCA、投影次梯度法和拉格朗日松弛的算法框架。

Result: 提出了一种高效解决非凸非光滑优化问题的方法，兼具理论严谨性和实际效果。

Conclusion: 新框架在语义感知资源分配中实现了高效且高质量的优化。

Abstract: The problem of resource allocation in goal-oriented semantic communication
with semantic-aware utilities and subjective risk perception is studied here.
By linking information importance to risk aversion, we model agent behavior
using Cumulative Prospect Theory (CPT), which incorporates risk-sensitive
utility functions and nonlinear transformations of distributions, reflecting
subjective perceptions of gains and losses. The objective is to maximize the
aggregate utility across multiple CPT-modeled agents, which leads to a
nonconvex, nonsmooth optimization problem. To efficiently solve this
challenging problem, we propose a new algorithmic framework that combines
successive convex approximation (SCA) with the projected subgradient method and
Lagrangian relaxation, Our approach enables tractable optimization while
preserving solution quality, offering both theoretical rigor and practical
effectiveness in semantics-aware resource allocation.

</details>


### [220] [CSI2Vec: Towards a Universal CSI Feature Representation for Positioning and Channel Charting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.05237)
*Victoria Palhares,Sueda Taner,Christoph Studer*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: CSI2Vec是一个自监督框架，用于生成通用的、鲁棒的信道状态信息（CSI）表示，适用于基于CSI的定位（POS）和信道图表（CC）。它通过学习紧凑的向量嵌入，捕捉用户设备之间的空间关系，无需依赖CSI重建或真实位置信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受Word2Vec等自然语言处理技术的启发，作者希望将类似的向量嵌入方法应用于无线通信领域，以解决CSI表示中的复杂性和效率问题。

Method: CSI2Vec通过神经网络学习不同无线场景下的紧凑向量嵌入，抽象化无线电设备和散射体的空间布置，以及硬件设置，从而生成通用的CSI表示。

Result: 仿真实验表明，CSI2Vec在保持出色的POS和CC性能的同时，显著降低了计算需求和存储开销。

Conclusion: CSI2Vec提供了一种高效且鲁棒的CSI表示方法，适用于多种无线场景，为下游任务提供了简化的处理流程。

Abstract: Natural language processing techniques, such as Word2Vec, have demonstrated
exceptional capabilities in capturing semantic and syntactic relationships of
text through vector embeddings. Inspired by this technique, we propose CSI2Vec,
a self-supervised framework for generating universal and robust channel state
information (CSI) representations tailored to CSI-based positioning (POS) and
channel charting (CC). CSI2Vec learns compact vector embeddings across various
wireless scenarios, capturing spatial relationships between user equipment
positions without relying on CSI reconstruction or ground-truth position
information. We implement CSI2Vec as a neural network that is trained across
various deployment setups (i.e., the spatial arrangement of radio equipment and
scatterers) and radio setups (RSs) (i.e., the specific hardware used), ensuring
robustness to aspects such as differences in the environment, the number of
used antennas, or allocated set of subcarriers. CSI2Vec abstracts the RS by
generating compact vector embeddings that capture essential spatial
information, avoiding the need for full CSI transmission or reconstruction
while also reducing complexity and improving processing efficiency of
downstream tasks. Simulations with ray-tracing and real-world CSI datasets
demonstrate CSI2Vec's effectiveness in maintaining excellent POS and CC
performance while reducing computational demands and storage.

</details>

### [221] [A model for the assembly map of bordism-invariant functors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.05238)
*Jordan Levin,Guglielmo Nocera,Victor Saunier*

Main category: math.KT

TL;DR: 研究了稳定范畴、厄米特范畴和庞加莱范畴的oplax余极限，构建了庞加莱范畴的装配映射的范畴模型，并推广了Shaneson分裂定理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索庞加莱范畴的装配映射及其在边界不变函子中的应用，推广现有理论以涵盖更广泛的情况。

Method: 利用oplax余极限构建范畴模型，并分析其核结构。

Result: 成功推广了Shaneson分裂定理，并解决了庞加莱-Verdier局部不变量的扭曲分裂问题。

Conclusion: 方法具有普适性，可应用于更广泛的范畴理论问题，并为相关领域提供了新的工具。

Abstract: We study oplax colimits of stable categories, of hermitian categories and of
Poincar\'e categories in nice cases. This allows us to produce a categorical
model of the assembly map of a bordism-invariant functor of Poincar\'e
categories which is also a Verdier projection, whose kernel we explicitly
describe. As a direct application, we generalize the Shaneson splitting for
bordism-invariant functors of Poincar\'e categories proved by
Calm\`es-Dotto-Harpaz-Hebestreit-Land-Moi-Nardin-Nikolaus-Steimle to allow for
twists. We also show our methods can tackle their general twisted Shaneson
splitting of Poincar\'e-Verdier localizing invariants which specifies to a
twisted Bass-Heller-Swan decomposition for the underlying stable categories,
generalizing part of recent work of Kirstein-Kremer.

</details>

### [223] [Nonstandard methods for ultrafilter relation extensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04692)
*Leonardo Raffaello Maximilian Gasparro,Lorenzo Luperi Baglini*

Main category: math.LO

  <summary>Details</summary>

whether various relation properties are preserved by these extensions. Lastly,
we study the notion of self-divisible ultrafilter and, with the mentioned

### [224] [The Aurellion Function: A Recursive Fast-Growing Hierarchy Beyond Knuth Notation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.05067)
*Daniel Vodrazka*

Main category: math.LO

TL;DR: 论文介绍了基于Knuth箭号表示法的Aurellion函数，分析了其相对于经典快速生长层级的增长速率，并讨论了其在形式算术中的可证明性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Aurellion函数的动机是探索一种新的快速生长层级，并将其与经典层级（如快速生长层级）进行比较，同时探讨其在形式算术中的可证明性。

Method: 通过递归定义Aurellion函数，使用Knuth箭号表示法，并分析其增长速率及与经典层级的比较。

Result: Aurellion函数的增长速率超过Peano算术中所有可证明总函数，且其能力接近证明论序数Γ₀。

Conclusion: Aurellion函数在符号大数构造和序数分析之间建立了桥梁，并展示了其强大的增长能力。

Abstract: We introduce the Aurellion Function, a novel recursively defined fast-growing
hierarchy based on Knuth's up-arrow notation, defined by $A_1 = 10
\uparrow\uparrow\uparrow 10$, $A_{n+1} = 10 \uparrow^{A_n} 10$, where the
number of arrows in the operation increases superexponentially with $n$. We
analyze its growth rate relative to classical hierarchies such as the
fast-growing hierarchy $(f_\alpha)_{\alpha < \varepsilon_0}$, and discuss its
provability status in formal arithmetic. We provide formal bounds showing $A_n$
dominates all functions provably total in Peano Arithmetic, situating the
Aurellion Function near the proof-theoretic ordinal $\Gamma_0$ due to its
ability to majorize all functions $f_\alpha$ for $\alpha < \varepsilon_0$. We
also outline possible transfinite extensions indexed by countable ordinals,
thus bridging symbolic large-number constructions and ordinal analysis.

</details>

### [227] [Estimating the Euclidean distortion of an orbit space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04425)
*Ben Blum-Smith,Harm Derksen,Dustin G. Mixon,Yousef Qaddura,Brantley Vose*

  <summary>Details</summary>

### [228] [Isoperimetric inequalities in Hadamard spaces of asymptotic rank two](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04882)
*Urs Lang,Stephan Stadler,David Urech*

Main category: math.MG

TL;DR: 证明了在具有有限线性控制渐近维度的空间中，维度≥2的一般循环满足同调不等式，适用于Hadamard 3-流形和有限维CAT(0)立方复合体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决Gromov关于Hadamard空间的等周间隙猜想，特别是在渐近秩为2的情况下，推广了Druţu-Lang-Papasoglu-Stadler的结果。

Method: 假设环境空间具有有限线性控制渐近维度，证明了一般循环的同调不等式。

Result: 在维度≥2的情况下，证明了同调不等式，适用于Hadamard 3-流形和有限维CAT(0)立方复合体。

Conclusion: 该研究扩展了等周不等式的适用范围，为高维Hadamard空间的理论提供了新的支持。

Abstract: Gromov's isoperimetric gap conjecture for Hadamard spaces states that cycles
in dimensions greater than or equal to the asymptotic rank admit linear
isoperimetric filling inequalities, as opposed to the inequalities of Euclidean
type in lower dimensions. In the case of asymptotic rank 2, recent progress was
made by Dru\c{t}u-Lang-Papasoglu-Stadler who established a homotopical
inequality for Lipschitz 2-spheres with exponents arbitrarily close to 1. We
prove a homological inequality of the same type for general cycles in
dimensions at least 2, assuming that the ambient space has finite linearly
controlled asymptotic dimension. This holds in particular for all Hadamard
3-manifolds and finite-dimensional CAT(0) cube complexes.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过数学证明和优化技术，改进面积上限。

Result: 证明了面积上限为$(1 - 2.6 \cdot 10^{-7}) \sqrt{2}$倍原凸体面积。

Conclusion: 研究显著改进了已知结果，为凸体几何提供了更优的理论支持。

Abstract: We show that every planar convex body is contained in a quadrangle whose area
is less than $(1 - 2.6 \cdot 10^{-7}) \sqrt{2}$ times the area of the original
convex body, improving the best known upper bound by W. Kuperberg.

### [233] [A New $q$-Heisenberg Algebra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04248)
*Julio Cesar Jaramillo Quiceno*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: Error


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Error

Method: Error

Result: Error

Conclusion: Error

Abstract: This work introduces a novel $q$-$\hbar$ deformation of the Heisenberg
algebra, designed to unify and extend several existing $q$-deformed
formulations. Starting from the canonical Heisenberg algebra defined by the
commutation relation $[\hat{x}, \hat{p}] = i\hbar$ on a Hilbert space
\cite{Zettili2009}, we survey a variety of $q$-deformed structures previously
proposed by Wess \cite{Wess2000}, Schm\"udgen \cite{Schmudgen1999},
Wess--Schwenk \cite{Wess-Schwenk1992}, Gaddis \cite{Jasson-Gaddis2016}, and
others. These frameworks involve position, momentum, and auxiliary operators
that satisfy nontrivial commutation rules and algebraic relations incorporating
deformation parameters. Our new $q$-$\hbar$ Heisenberg algebra $\mathcal{H}_q$
is generated by elements $\hat{x}_\alpha$, $\hat{y}_\lambda$, and
$\hat{p}_\beta$ with $\alpha, \lambda, \beta \in \{1,2,3\}$, and is defined
through generalized commutation relations parameterized by real constants $n,
m, l$ and three dynamical functions $\Psi(q)$, $\Phi(q)$, and $\Pi(q)$
depending on the deformation parameter $q$ and the generators. By selecting
appropriate values for these parameters and functions, our framework recovers
several well-known algebras as special cases, including the classical
Heisenberg algebra for $q = 1$ and $\Psi = 1$, $\Phi = \Pi = 0$, and various
$q$-deformed algebras for $q \neq 1$. The algebraic consistency of these
generalizations is demonstrated through a series of explicit examples, and the
resulting structures are shown to align with quantum planes
\cite{Yuri-Manin2010} and enveloping algebras associated with Lie algebra
homomorphisms \cite{Reyes2014a}. This construction offers a flexible and
unified formalism for studying quantum deformations, with potential
applications in quantum mechanics, noncommutative geometry, and quantum group
theory.

### [234] [Is Crane--Yetter fully extended?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04864)
*Luuk Stehouwer*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 论文探讨了Crane-Yetter拓扑量子场论（TQFT）是否支持完全扩展的细化，利用稳定同伦理论对四维可逆TQFT进行分类，并发现其扩展由两个数据决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Crane-Yetter TQFT的完全扩展性，澄清文献中的常见说法，并探讨如何自然选择特定数据以匹配Crane-Yetter状态和。

Method: 使用稳定同伦理论工具，对可逆四维TQFT进行分类，分析其在对称单oidal 4-范畴中的扩展。

Result: 发现扩展由可逆对象等价类和六次单位根决定，并在Braided Fusion范畴中验证了无限多等价类的存在。

Abstract: We revisit the question of whether the Crane-Yetter topological quantum field
theory (TQFT) associated to a modular tensor category admits a fully extended
refinement. More specifically, we use tools from stable homotopy theory to
classify extensions of invertible four-dimensional TQFTs to theories valued in
symmetric monoidal 4-categories whose Picard spectrum has nontrivial homotopy
only in degrees 0 and 4. We show that such extensions are classified by two
pieces of data: an equivalence class of an invertible object in the target and
a sixth root of unity. Applying this result to the 4-category $\mathbf{BrFus}$
of braided fusion categories, we find that there are infinitely many
equivalence classes of fully extended invertible TQFTs reproducing the
Crane-Yetter partition function on top-dimensional manifolds, parametrized by a
$\mathbb{Z}/6$-extension of the Witt group of nondegenerate braided fusion
categories.
  This analysis clarifies common claims in the literature and raises the
question of how to naturally pick out the $SO(4)$-fixed point data on the
framed TQFT which assigns the input braided fusion category to the point so
that it selects the Crane-Yetter state-sum.

### [235] [Conformal nets from minimal W-algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04270)
*Sebastiano Carpi,Tiziano Gaudio*

Result: 证明了所有强有理酉极小W-代数对应已知的完全有理分级局部共形网，并验证了N=0-4超Virasoro顶点超代数的猜想。

*Jorge R. Bolaños-Servín,Roberto Quezada,Josué I. Rios-Cangas*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用Yosida近似定义ρ-可积性，分析生成的交换*-代数性质，建立范数并推导关键公式。

Result: 证明了生成的代数元素正规且ρ-可积，协方差算子S具有实数、有界、正定、可逆且满足S−iJ≥0的性质。

Conclusion: 方法严格定义了量子高斯态的数学性质，为相关研究提供了理论基础和工具。

Abstract: We develop an analytical approach to quantum Gaussian states in infinite-mode
representation of the Canonical Commutation Relations (CCR's), using Yosida
approximations to define integrability of possibly unbounded observables with
respect to a state $\rho$ ($\rho$-integrability). It turns out that all
elements of the commutative $*$-algebra generated by a possibly unbounded
$\rho$-integrable observable $A$, denoted by $\langle A\rangle$, are normal and
$\rho \, $-integrable. Besides, $\langle A\rangle$ can be endowed with the
well-defined norm $\|\cdot\|_\rho:= {\rm tr}\,(\rho |\cdot| )$. Our approach
allows us to rigorously establish fundamental properties and derive key
formulae for the mean value vector and the covariance operator. We additionally
show that the covariance operator $S$ of any Gaussian state is real, bounded,
positive, and invertible, with the property that $S-iJ\geq 0$, being $J$ the
multiplication operator by $-i$ on $\ell_2({\mathbb N})$.

### [237] [Very high-order accurate finite volume scheme for the streamfunction-vorticity formulation of incompressible fluid flows with polygonal meshes on arbitrary curved boundaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.05081)
*Ricardo Costa,Stéphane Clain,Gaspar J. Machado,João M. Nóbrega*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种高效的二维不可压缩Navier-Stokes方程的高阶有限体积离散方法，基于流函数-涡量公式，避免了压力-速度耦合问题，并解决了边界条件处理的挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于压力和速度的Navier-Stokes方程模拟存在压力-速度耦合问题，而流函数-涡量公式虽避免了这一问题，但边界条件处理困难。本文旨在解决这一挑战。

Method: 采用高阶有限体积离散方法处理流函数-涡量公式，通过重构边界附近数据的方法避免复杂曲线网格生成，同时保持高收敛阶。

Result: 在复杂二维曲线域中的不可压缩流体流动测试中，该方法展示了高精度和高收敛阶的有效性。

Conclusion: 提出的方法在流函数-涡量公式中高效解决了边界条件问题，适用于复杂几何域的高精度模拟。

Abstract: Conventional mathematical models for simulating incompressible fluid flow
problems are based on the Navier-Stokes equations expressed in terms of
pressure and velocity. In this context, pressure-velocity coupling is a key
issue, and countless numerical techniques and methods have been developed over
the decades to solve these equations efficiently and accurately. In two
dimensions, an alternative approach is to rewrite the Navier-Stokes equations
regarding two scalar quantities: the streamfunction and the vorticity. Compared
to the primitive variables approach, this formulation does not require pressure
to be computed, thereby avoiding the inherent difficulties associated with the
pressure-velocity coupling. However, deriving boundary conditions for the
streamfunction and vorticity is challenging. This work proposes an efficient,
high-order accurate finite-volume discretisation of the two-dimensional
incompressible Navier-Stokes equations in the streamfunction-vorticity
formulation. A detailed discussion is devoted to deriving the appropriate
boundary conditions and their numerical treatment, including on arbitrary
curved boundaries. The reconstruction for off-site data method is employed to
avoid the difficulties associated with generating curved meshes to preserve
high-orders of convergence in arbitrary curved domains, such as sophisticated
meshing algorithms, cumbersome quadrature rules, and intricate non-linear
transformations. This method approximates arbitrary curved boundaries with a
conventional linear piecewise approximation, while constrained polynomial
reconstructions near the boundary fulfil the prescribed conditions at the
physical boundary. Several incompressible fluid flow test cases in non-trivial
2D curved domains are presented and discussed to demonstrate the accuracy and
effectiveness of the proposed methodology in achieving very high orders of
convergence.

</details>

### [240] [A New $q$-Heisenberg Algebra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04248)
*Julio Cesar Jaramillo Quiceno*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: Error


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Error

Method: Error

Result: Error

Conclusion: Error

Abstract: This work introduces a novel $q$-$\hbar$ deformation of the Heisenberg
algebra, designed to unify and extend several existing $q$-deformed
formulations. Starting from the canonical Heisenberg algebra defined by the
commutation relation $[\hat{x}, \hat{p}] = i\hbar$ on a Hilbert space
\cite{Zettili2009}, we survey a variety of $q$-deformed structures previously
proposed by Wess \cite{Wess2000}, Schm\"udgen \cite{Schmudgen1999},
Wess--Schwenk \cite{Wess-Schwenk1992}, Gaddis \cite{Jasson-Gaddis2016}, and
others. These frameworks involve position, momentum, and auxiliary operators
that satisfy nontrivial commutation rules and algebraic relations incorporating
deformation parameters. Our new $q$-$\hbar$ Heisenberg algebra $\mathcal{H}_q$
is generated by elements $\hat{x}_\alpha$, $\hat{y}_\lambda$, and
$\hat{p}_\beta$ with $\alpha, \lambda, \beta \in \{1,2,3\}$, and is defined
through generalized commutation relations parameterized by real constants $n,
m, l$ and three dynamical functions $\Psi(q)$, $\Phi(q)$, and $\Pi(q)$
depending on the deformation parameter $q$ and the generators. By selecting
appropriate values for these parameters and functions, our framework recovers
several well-known algebras as special cases, including the classical
Heisenberg algebra for $q = 1$ and $\Psi = 1$, $\Phi = \Pi = 0$, and various
$q$-deformed algebras for $q \neq 1$. The algebraic consistency of these
generalizations is demonstrated through a series of explicit examples, and the
resulting structures are shown to align with quantum planes
\cite{Yuri-Manin2010} and enveloping algebras associated with Lie algebra
homomorphisms \cite{Reyes2014a}. This construction offers a flexible and
unified formalism for studying quantum deformations, with potential
applications in quantum mechanics, noncommutative geometry, and quantum group
theory.

theories in lower dimensions. We also consider multiple descent along pairwise
commuting vector fields of invariance, yielding a finer decomposition of
Maxwell's equations. Our results provide a unified and geometrically
transparent interpretation of dimensional reduction, with potential
applications to field theories in lower-dimensional spacetimes.

</details>

### [247] [On the finite generation of the cohomology of bosonizations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.05267)

algebras (such as Nichols algebras of diagonal type, the restricted Jordan

examples.

### [249] [Green functions for positive-depth Deligne--Lusztig induction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04449)
*Charlotte Chan,Masao Oi*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 论文在剩余域较大的假设下，明确描述了非分歧椭圆对$(T,\theta)$的正深度Deligne--Lusztig诱导。当$\theta$正则时，该诱导实现了Kaletha的Howe-非分歧正则$L$-包。通过简单的“litmus test”定理，推导出未来可能的应用。此外，论文还比较了Yu构造与几何诱导的Green函数，并证明了正深度Springer假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究非分歧椭圆对的正深度Deligne--Lusztig诱导，以几何方式实现Kaletha的$L$-包，并为小$p$构造提供潜在应用。

Method: 利用剩余域较大的假设，通过“litmus test”定理描述诱导；比较Yu构造与几何诱导的Green函数；推导正深度Springer假设。

Result: 正深度Deligne--Lusztig诱导实现了Kaletha的$L$-包；Green函数的比较结果；正深度Springer假设的证明。

Conclusion: 论文为正深度Deligne--Lusztig诱导提供了明确描述，并展示了其在几何实现和比较问题中的应用潜力。

Abstract: Under a largeness assumption on the size of the residue field, we give an
explicit description of the positive-depth Deligne--Lusztig induction of
unramified elliptic pairs $(T,\theta)$. When $\theta$ is regular, we show that
positive-depth Deligne--Lusztig induction gives a geometric realization of
Kaletha's Howe-unramified regular $L$-packets. This is obtained as an immediate
corollary of a very simple "litmus test" characterization theorem which we
foresee will have interesting future applications to small-$p$ constructions.
We next define and analyze Green functions of two different origins: Yu's
construction (algebra) and positive-depth Deligne--Lusztig induction
(geometry). Using this, we deduce a comparison result for arbitrary $\theta$
from the regular setting. As a further application of our comparison
isomorphism, we prove the positive-depth Springer hypothesis in the $0$-toral
setting and use it to give a geometric explanation for the appearance of
orbital integrals in supercuspidal character formulae.

</details>

### [253] [Pólya's conjecture on $\mathbb{S}^1 \times \R$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04341)
*Pedro Freitas,Rui Wang*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 研究了无限圆柱上两种可能的等周域（测地圆盘和圆柱带）满足Pólya猜想时的面积范围。前者给出了半径上限，后者完全刻画了满足条件的h值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨无限圆柱上等周域的性质及其与Pólya猜想的关系。

Method: 分析测地圆盘和圆柱带的面积范围，分别给出半径上限和h值的完全刻画。

Result: 确定了满足Pólya猜想的等周域的必要充分条件，并给出了圆柱带上Li-Yau不等式成立的类似条件。

Conclusion: 为无限圆柱上的等周问题提供了理论支持，并扩展了对Pólya猜想和Li-Yau不等式的理解。

Abstract: We study the area ranges where the two possible isoperimetric domains on the
infinite cylinder $\mathbb{S}^{1}\times \R$, namely, geodesic disks and
cylindrical strips of the form $\mathbb{S}^1\times [0,h]$, satisfy P\'{o}lya's
conjecture. In the former case, we provide an upper bound on the maximum value
of the radius for which the conjecture may hold, while in the latter we fully
characterise the values of $h$ for which it does hold for these strips. As a
consequence, we determine a necessary and sufficient condition for the
isoperimetric domain on $\mathbb{S}^{1}\times \R$ corresponding to a given area
to satisfy P\'{o}lya's conjecture. In the case of the cylindrical strip, we
also provide a necessary and sufficient condition for the Li-Yau inequalities
to hold.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Accurately identifying the extremal dependence structure in multivariate

Chinese A-share stocks over a time period well before the U.S. election in
2024. The procedure reveals more isolated clustering of dependent assets in the
U.S. economy compared with China which exhibits different characteristics and a
more interconnected pattern of extremal dependence. Cross-market analysis
identifies strong extremal linkages in sectors such as materials, consumer
staples and consumer discretionary, highlighting the effectiveness of the
testing procedure for large-scale empirical applications.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: In recent years, a variety of novel measures of dependence have been
introduced being capable of characterizing diverse types of directed
dependence, hence diverse types of how a number of predictor variables
$\mathbf{X} = (X_1, \dots, X_p)$, $p \in \mathbb{N}$, may affect a response
variable $Y$. This includes perfect dependence of $Y$ on $\mathbf{X}$ and
independence between $\mathbf{X}$ and $Y$, but also less well-known concepts
such as zero-explainability, stochastic comparability and complete separation.
Certain such measures offer a representation in terms of the Markov product
$(Y,Y')$, with $Y'$ being a conditionally independent copy of $Y$ given
$\mathbf{X}$. This dimension reduction principle allows these measures to be
estimated via the powerful nearest neighbor based estimation principle
introduced in [4]. To achieve a deeper insight into the dimension reduction
principle, this paper aims at translating the extreme variants of directed
dependence, typically formulated in terms of the random vector
$(\mathbf{X},Y)$, into the Markov product $(Y,Y')$.
